20Curing ImoutoBy doing "Drink something together.",
you can let your sister drink the Philosopher's Stone Fragment that has turned into a liquid

PS: Currently, it can only cure the sister twice. As to how to obtain this item, please refer to the RPG section of this guide document		Forcibly waking up imouto will no longer occur.

After being cured, there is a chance to successfully wake her up in the morning to trigger some scenes such as toothbrushing. However, there's still a chance of failure in waking her up.

First cure:
You can stay up late until 22:30. After the first wake-up event in the morning, there is a 50% chance to successfully wake up imouto

Second cure:
You can stay up late until 23:00. After the first wake-up event in the morning, there is a 75% chance to successfully wake up imouto

Third cure (not yet implemented)
You can stay up late until 00:00. After the first wake-up event in the morning, there is a 100% chance to successfully wake up imouto
